<
    opset_imports={'': 18},
>
def com.qti.aisw.onnx::CustomRMSNorm(
    inputs=(
        %"hidden_states"<?,?>,
        %"weight"<?,?>
    ),
    attributes={
        epsilon: UNDEFINED
    }
    outputs=(
        %"return_val"<FLOAT,[]>
    ),
) {
     0 |  # n0
          %"weight_0"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Cast(%"weight") {to=1}
     1 |  # n1
          %"int64_2"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Constant() {value=TensorProtoTensor<INT64,[]>(array(2), name='int64_2')}
     2 |  # n2
          %"tmp"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Pow(%"hidden_states", %"int64_2")
     3 |  # n3
          %"int64_m1_1d"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Constant() {value=TensorProtoTensor<INT64,[1]>(array([-1]), name='int64_m1_1d')}
     4 |  # n4
          %"variance"<?,?> ⬅️ ::ReduceMean(%"tmp", %"int64_m1_1d") {keepdims=1}
     5 |  # n5
          %"epsilon"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Constant() {value_float=@epsilon}
     6 |  # n6
          %"tmp_1"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Shape(%"variance")
     7 |  # n7
          %"epsilon_2"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Expand(%"epsilon", %"tmp_1")
     8 |  # n8
          %"tmp_3"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Add(%"variance", %"epsilon_2")
     9 |  # n9
          %"tmp_4"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Sqrt(%"tmp_3")
    10 |  # n10
          %"tmp_5"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Reciprocal(%"tmp_4")
    11 |  # n11
          %"hidden_states_6"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Mul(%"hidden_states", %"tmp_5")
    12 |  # n12
          %"return_val"<FLOAT,[]> ⬅️ ::Mul(%"weight_0", %"hidden_states_6")
    return %"return_val"<FLOAT,[]>
}

<
    opset_imports={'': 18},
>
def com.qualcomm.cloud::CtxScatter(
    inputs=(
        %"data"<?,?>,
        %"position_ids"<?,?>,
        %"updates"<?,?>
    ),
    outputs=(
        %"return_val"<FLOAT,[]>
    ),
) {
     0 |  # n0
          %"tmp"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Shape(%"data")
     1 |  # n1
          %"int64_0_1d"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Constant() {value=TensorProtoTensor<INT64,[1]>(array([0]), name='int64_0_1d')}
     2 |  # n2
          %"batch_size"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Gather(%"tmp", %"int64_0_1d")
     3 |  # n3
          %"tmp_0"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Shape(%"data")
     4 |  # n4
          %"int64_1_1d"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Constant() {value=TensorProtoTensor<INT64,[1]>(array([1]), name='int64_1_1d')}
     5 |  # n5
          %"num_heads"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Gather(%"tmp_0", %"int64_1_1d")
     6 |  # n6
          %"tmp_1"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Shape(%"position_ids")
     7 |  # n7
          %"int64_1_1d_2"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Constant() {value=TensorProtoTensor<INT64,[1]>(array([1]), name='int64_1_1d_2')}
     8 |  # n8
          %"seq_len"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Gather(%"tmp_1", %"int64_1_1d_2")
     9 |  # n9
          %"zero"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Constant() {value_ints=(0,)}
    10 |  # n10
          %"one"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Constant() {value_ints=(1,)}
    11 |  # n11
          %"exp_shape"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Concat(%"batch_size", %"num_heads", %"seq_len", %"one") {axis=0}
    12 |  # n12
          %"tmp_3"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Range(%"zero", %"batch_size", %"one")
    13 |  # n13
          %"const"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Constant() {value=TensorProtoTensor<INT64,[3]>(array([1, 2, 3]), name='const')}
    14 |  # n14
          %"tmp_4"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Unsqueeze(%"tmp_3", %"const")
    15 |  # n15
          %"batch_idx"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Expand(%"tmp_4", %"exp_shape")
    16 |  # n16
          %"tmp_5"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Range(%"zero", %"num_heads", %"one")
    17 |  # n17
          %"const_6"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Constant() {value=TensorProtoTensor<INT64,[3]>(array([0, 2, 3]), name='const_6')}
    18 |  # n18
          %"tmp_7"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Unsqueeze(%"tmp_5", %"const_6")
    19 |  # n19
          %"head_idx"<?,?> ⬅️ ::Expand(%"tmp_7", %"exp_shape")
    20 |  # n20
